⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
(۸۳۳) واحـكـام الاضحى كالفطر لكنه في الاضحى يؤخر الاكل عن الصلوة ويكبر في الطريق جهرا و يعلم معه بلال فأمرهن بالصدقة فجعلن يلقين ، تلقى المرأة خرصها و سخابها ۔ ( بخاری شریف، باب الخطبة بعد العيد، ص ۱۵۵، نمبر ۱۹۶۴ مسلم شریف ، باب کتاب صلوۃ العیدین ، ص ۱۳۵۴، نمبر ۲۰۴۵/۸۸۴) اس حدیث میں نماز کے بعد صدقہ فطر کے احکام عورتوں کو بتایا۔ ترجمه : ... (۸۳۳) اور عیدالاضحی کے احکام عید الفطر کی طرح ہیں، مگر یہ کہ عید الاضحی میں کھانا نماز سے مؤخر کرے، اور راستے میں تكبیر زور سے کہے، اور خطبہ میں قربانی کے احکام اور تكبیر تشریق سکھلائے۔ اور عذر کی وجہ سے تین دن تک مؤخر کر سکتا ہے۔ تشریح : عید الاضحی کے احکام عید الفطر کی طرح ہیں، البتہ ان چار احکام میں فرق ہے۔[1] عیدالفطر میں نماز سے پہلے کھانا سنت ہے، اور بقر عید میں نماز کے بعد کھانا سنت ہے [۲] عید الفطر میں راستے میں آہستہ تکبیر کہنا سنت ہے، اور بقر عید میں زور سے تکبیر کہنا سنت ہے ۔ [۳] عید الفطر میں خطبہ میں عید الفطر کے احکام سکھائے ، اور بقر عید میں خطبہ میں قربانی کے احکام سکھائے [۴] عذر ہو تو عید الفطر میں نماز ایک دن مؤخر کر سکتا ہے اور بقر عید میں تین دن تک مؤخر کر سکتا ہے۔ وجه : (۱) عید الاضحیٰ میں نماز کے بعد کھا نا سنت ہے اس کی دلیل یہ حدیث ہے۔ عن عبد الله بن بريدة عن ابيه قال كان النبي الله لا يخرج يوم الفطر حتى يطعم ، و لا يطعم يوم الاضحى حتى يصلى ( ترمذی شریف، باب ماجاء فی الاکل یوم الفطر قبل الخروج ، ص ۱۴۲، نمبر ۵۴۲ / ابن ماجہ شریف ، باب فی الاکل یوم الفطر قبل ان يخرج ، ص ۲۵۰، نمبر ۱۷۵۶) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ عید الفطر میں نماز سے پہلے اور عید الاضحیٰ میں نماز کے بعد کھایا کرتے تھے۔ (۲) اور قربانی کے گوشت کو ہی کھائے اسکی دلیل یہ حدیث ہے۔ حدثنا عبد الله بن بريدة عن أبيه : أن النبي الله كان لا يخرج يوم الفطر حتى يطعم ، و كان لا يأكل يوم النحر شيئا حتى يرجع فيأكل من أضحيته ( دارقطني ، كتاب العیدین ج ثانی ص ۳۴ نمبر ۶۹۹ ارسنن للبيهقي ، باب بيترك الاكل يوم النحر حتى يرجع ، ج ثالث ، ص ۴۰۱، نمبر ۶۱۶ ) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ قربانی کے گوشت سے افطاری کرنا زیادہ بہتر ہے۔ (۳) عن ابن عمر أنه اذا غدا يوم الاضحى ويوم الفطر يجهر بالتكبير حتى يأتى المصلى ، ثم يكبر حتى يأتى الامام - (دار قطنی، کتاب العیدین ج ثانی ص ۳۴ نمبر ۷۰۰ار مصنف ابن ابی شیبۃ ، باب ۱۳)، فی التکبیر اذا خرج الی العید ، ج اول ص ۷ ۴۸ نمبر ۵۶۱۸) اس اثر سے معلوم ہوا کہ عید الفطر اور عیدالاضحیٰ دونوں کے راستے میں تکبیر زور سے کہی جائے گی۔ (۴) بقر عید کے خطبے میں قربانی کے احکام سکھلائے ۔ عن البراء قال : خطبنا النبي الله يوم النحر فقال ان اول ما نبدأ به في يومنا هذا أن نصلى ثم نرجع فننحر ، فمن فعل ذالک فقد اصاب سنتنا۔ ( بخاری شریف ، باب التکبیر للعید ، ص ۱۵۵، نمبر ۱۹۶۸ مسلم شریف ، باب کتاب الاضاحی ، باب وقتها ،ص ۸۷۵، نمبر ۱۹۶۱ار ۵۰۷۱) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ بقر عید کے موقع پر خطبہ دیا تو قربانی کے احکام بیان فرمائے۔(۵) اور عذر کی بنا پر تین دن تک مؤخر اس لئے کر سکتا ہے کہ تین دن تک قربانی کر سکتا ہے تو تین دن تک نماز بھی پڑھ سکتا ہے۔
(833) And the rules of Eid al-Adha are like those of Eid al-Fitr, except that on Eid al-Adha he delays eating until after the prayer, and he says the takbir loudly on the way, and he teaches with him (?) ... (hadith) ... In this hadith, the rules of sadaqat al-fitr after the prayer were taught to the women. Translation: ... (833) And the rules of Eid al-Adha are like those of Eid al-Fitr, except that on Eid al-Adha he delays eating until after the prayer, and he says the takbir loudly on the way, and in the khutbah he teaches the rules of sacrifice and takbir al-tashriq. And he may delay due to an excuse until three days. Commentary: The rules of Eid al-Adha are like those of Eid al-Fitr; however, there is a difference in these four rules. [1] On Eid al-Fitr, eating before the prayer is sunnah, and on Eid al-Adha, eating after the prayer is sunnah. [2] On Eid al-Fitr, saying the takbir softly on the way is sunnah, and on Eid al-Adha, saying it loudly is sunnah. [3] On Eid al-Fitr, the khutbah teaches the rules of Eid al-Fitr, and on Eid al-Adha, the khutbah teaches the rules of sacrifice. [4] If there is an excuse, on Eid al-Fitr the prayer can be delayed one day, and on Eid al-Adha up to three days. Reason: (1) The evidence that it is sunnah to eat after the prayer on Eid al-Adha is this hadith from 'Abdullah ibn Buraidah from his father: The Prophet would not go out on the day of Fitr until he had eaten, and he would not eat on the day of Adha until he had prayed. (Tirmidhi, Bab ma Ja'a fi al-Akl Yawm al-Fitr Qabl al-Khuruj, p. 142, #542; Ibn Majah, Bab fi al-Akl Yawm al-Fitr Qabl an Yakhruj, p. 250, #1756) (2) And he should eat from the meat of the sacrifice; evidence: the hadith from Ibn Buraidah: The Prophet would not go out on Fitr until he ate, and on the day of Nahr he would not eat anything until he returned and ate from his sacrifice. (Daraqutni, Kitab al-'Eedayn, Vol. 2, p. 34, #699; Bayhaqi, Bab Yatruku al-Akl Yawm al-Nahr Hatta Yarj'u, Vol. 3, p. 401, #616) (3) Ibn 'Umar would go out on the day of Adha and the day of Fitr and raise his voice with takbir until he reached the musalla, then continue until the imam came. (Daraqutni, Kitab al-'Eedayn, Vol. 2, p. 34, #700; Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah, Bab 13 fi al-Takbir Itha Kharaja ila al-'Eed, Vol. 1, p. 748, #5618) (4) On the Eid al-Adha, the khutbah teaches the rules of sacrifice: Al-Bara' said: The Prophet delivered a khutbah on the day of Nahr and said: The first thing we begin with on this day is to pray, then we return and sacrifice. Whoever does that has followed our sunnah. (Bukhari, Bab al-Takbir li al-'Eed, p. 155, #1968; Muslim, Kitab al-Adahi, Bab Waqtuha, p. 875, #1961/5071) (5) And the reason it can be delayed up to three days due to excuse is that the sacrifice can be performed up to three days, so the prayer can also be performed up to three days.
Source pages p. 91

Commentary
This passage is a detailed comparison of the rules of Eid al-Adha and Eid al-Fitr. The author states four specific differences, each supported by hadith. First, the timing of eating: on Fitr it is sunnah to eat before the prayer, while on Adha it is sunnah to eat after the prayer, based on the hadith of Ibn Buraidah. Second, the manner of takbir: on Fitr it is said softly, while on Adha it is said loudly, based on the practice of Ibn 'Umar. Third, the content of the khutbah: each khutbah covers the specific rulings of that Eid. Fourth, the allowance for delay: Fitr can be delayed one day, Adha up to three days, because the days of tashriq extend to three days. All these rulings are grounded in the sunnah.

Key Terms
تلبية (talbiyah): Not present in this passage but related to takbir.
تكبير التشريق (takbīr al-tashrīq): The takbir recited after fard prayers from Fajr of 9th Dhul Hijjah to Asr of 13th.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
On which Eid is it sunnah to eat before the prayer?
A) Eid al-Adha
B) Eid al-Fitr
C) Both
D) Neither

Key Takeaway
The four sunnah differences between Eid al-Adha and Eid al-Fitr are established by clear hadith and should be observed to follow the Prophet's practice.

Takbir al-Tashriq: A Wajib Act with Conditions
Ruling on Takbir al-Tashriq and its conditions

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the ruling of Takbir al-Tashriq as wajib in the Hanafi school, identify the conditions that make it obligatory, and distinguish the Hanafi position from other madhhabs.

Core Idea
Takbir al-Tashriq is wajib after every congregational fard prayer during the days of tashriq—but only if the imam is a resident.

This lesson presents the Hanafi ruling on Takbir al-Tashriq, a special takbir recited after certain prayers during the days of Hajj. According to Imam Abu Hanifah, it is not merely a sunnah but a wajib (obligatory) act, though with specific conditions. Understanding these conditions is key to correct practice.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
Examine the text to determine what act is being ruled upon (Takbir al-Tashriq) and the level of obligation (wajib).
Wajib means obligatory; omission without excuse is sinful.
2
Determine the time frame
Note the time period: from Fajr of 9th Dhul Hijjah (Yawm 'Arafah) to Asr of 13th Dhul Hijjah (end of Tashriq days).
There are 23 prayers during this period if one includes all fard prayers.
3
List the conditions for obligation
The text specifies three conditions: (1) it is recited after a fard prayer, (2) that prayer is performed in congregation, and (3) the imam is a resident of the city (muqim).
The follower may be a traveler, slave, or woman, as long as the imam is resident.
4
Note the intra-madhhab ikhtilaf
Imam Abu Hanifah considers it wajib, while his students Abu Yusuf and Muhammad consider it sunnah mu'akkadah. The relied-upon (mufta bihi) position is that of Imam Abu Hanifah.
This difference does not affect the basic practice, only the weight of obligation.
5
Apply the ruling to a scenario
Consider a case where a person prays fard alone at home during the days of Tashriq. Since the condition of congregation is not met, Takbir al-Tashriq is not wajib upon that person.
If any condition is missing, the takbir is not wajib; it may still be recited as a good deed.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
(۸۳۵) ويجب التشريـق مـن بـعـد فجر عرفة الى عصر العيد مرة فور كل فرض أُدّى بجماعة (على الإمام الذي في المصر والمأموم ولو مسافراً أو عبداً أو امرأة عند الإمام أبي حنيفة) (۸۳۵) تكبیر تشریق واجب ہے یوم عرفہ کے فجر کے بعد سے عید کے عصر تک ایک مرتبہ ہر فرض نماز کے بعد جو مستحب جماعت کے ساتھ ادا کی گئی ہو امام پر جو شہر میں مقیم ہو اور اس پر جس نے اس کی اقتداء کی ہے۔ چاہے مسافر ہو، یا غلام ہو، یا عورت ہو امام ابوحنیفہ کے نزدیک۔
(835) And takbir al-tashriq is wajib from after the Fajr of 'Arafah (9th Dhul Hijjah) until the Asr of the 'Eid (13th Dhul Hijjah), once after every fard prayer performed in congregation (upon the imam who is in the city, and upon the follower even if he is a traveler, a slave, or a woman according to Imam Abu Hanifah).
Source pages p. 92

Commentary
This is a ruling on Takbir al-Tashriq. According to Imam Abu Hanifah, it is wajib to recite the takbir once after every fard prayer that is performed in congregation during the days of tashriq (from Fajr of the 9th to Asr of the 13th of Dhul Hijjah). This obligation applies to the imam who is a resident of the city, and also to those who follow him in prayer, regardless of whether they are travelers, slaves, or women. The takbir is wajib only after fard prayers prayed with an imam who is a resident; if one prays alone or the imam is a traveler, the takbir is not wajib. This is specific to the Hanafi school, as other schools may consider it sunnah rather than wajib.

Key Terms
تكبير التشريق (takbīr al-tashrīq): The specified takbir recited after fard prayers from Fajr of 9th Dhul Hijjah to Asr of 13th Dhul Hijjah.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to Imam Abu Hanifah, after which prayers must Takbir al-Tashriq be recited?
A) After every prayer, fard or nafl
B) After every fard prayer performed in congregation
C) Only after the Eid prayer
D) After every prayer recited in the masjid

Key Takeaway
Takbir al-Tashriq is a wajib act in the Hanafi school after every congregational fard prayer during the specified days, with the condition that the imam is a resident.

Takbir al-Tashriq: Intra-Hanafi Dispute on Conditions
States the obligation of takbir al-tashriq and the intra-Hanafi dispute on its conditions

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the two Hanafi positions on the obligation of takbir al-tashriq, identify their proofs, and explain which position is mufta bihi and why.

Core Idea
Takbir al-tashriq is wajib for all after every fard prayer, according to the relied-upon Hanafi view.

In this passage from Thamaratun Najah, we learn about takbir al-tashriq—the recitation of Allahu Akbar during the days of Tashriq. The Hanafi school unanimously considers it wajib, but there is an intra-madhhab dispute regarding its conditions. Imam Abu Hanifa restricts it to congregational prayers in cities, while the Sahibayn extend it to everyone after every fard prayer. The text explains both views and their proofs, then declares the Sahibayn's view as the operative position.

Guided Path
1
Identify the two positions on takbir al-tashriq
From the passage, extract the conditions stipulated by Imam Abu Hanifa (congregation, city, imam/ma'mum) and by the Sahibayn (no restrictions). Note the time frames: Abu Hanifa says from Fajr of Arafa to Asr of Eid (10th); Sahibayn from Fajr of Arafa to Asr of 13th.
The time difference is minor; the key is the conditions of obligation.
2
Examine the dalil for each view
Look at the companion statements cited: Abu Hanifa relies on the statement of Ali (RA) linking takbir to a major city (misr jami'). The Sahibayn rely on the general practice of Ibn Mas'ud and Ibrahim al-Nakha'i who said to recite it whether alone or in congregation. Note the sources (Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah).
Both use athar (companion reports) – the difference is in interpretation of generality.
3
Analyze the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical difference: Under Abu Hanifa's view, a person praying alone in a village does not recite takbir. Under the Sahibayn's view, that same person must recite. This affects travelers, women praying at home, and those in rural areas.
This shows the real-world impact of the dispute.
4
Determine the tarjih
The passage explicitly states 'alayhi al-amal wa al-fatwa' for the Sahibayn's view. This means the later Hanafi masters relied on this position. Understand why: it is based on broader evidence and easier adherence.
The tarjih is based on practice and fatwa, not necessarily superiority of proof.
5
Confirm the hukm level
Both positions agree it is wajib (not fard). The passage explains that the proof is from ahad hadith and athar, not Quran or mutawatir, so it does not reach the level of fard.
This illustrates the Hanafi distinction between fard and wajib based on certainty of proof.

تعریف منانا کہتے ہیں ۔ اس کی کوئی حیثیت اس لئے نہیں ہے کہ یہ سب میدان عرفات میں عبادت ہیں دوسری جگہ ان کی کوئی حیثیت نہیں ہے۔ ترجمه : (۸۳۵) تکبیر تشریق واجب ہے یوم عرفہ کے فجر کے بعد سے عید کے عصر تک ایک مرتبہ ہر فرض نماز کے بعد جو مستحب جماعت کے ساتھ ادا کی گئی ہو امام پر جو شہر میں مقیم ہو اور اس پر جس نے اس کی اقتداء کی ہے۔ چاہے مسافر ہو، یا غلام ہو، یا عورت ہو امام ابوحنیفہ کے نزدیک۔ تشریح : نویں ذی الحجہ کے فجر سے تیرہویں ذی الحجہ کے عصر تک جو نماز مستحب جماعت کے ساتھ ادا کی گئی ہو اس کے امام پر اور اس کے مقتدی پر ایک مرتبہ تکبیر تشریق کہے۔ چاہے مسافر ہو چاہے غلام ہو یا عورت ہوسب پر واجب ہے۔ اور اکیلا پڑھی ہو تو تکبیر پڑھنا واجب نہیں ہے۔ وجه (۱) تکبیر تشریق کا ثبوت اس آیت میں ہے . ويذكر وا اسم الله فی ایام معلومات على ما رزقهم من بهيمة الانعام ۔ ( آیت ۲۸ ،سورۃ الحج ۲۲) اس آیت میں جواللہ کا ذکر کرنے کے لئے کہا گیا ہے اس میں تکبیر تشریق بھی ہے۔ (۲) اس قول صحابی میں بھی اس کا ذکر . و كـان عـمـر يـكـبـر فـي قبـة بـمـنـي فيسمعه أهل المسجد فيكبرون و يكبر أهل الاسواق حتى ترتج منى تكبيرا و كان ابن عمر يكبر بمنی تلک الايام و خلف الصلوات ۔ ( بخاری شریف باب التکبیر ایام منی واذ اغدا الی عرفته ص ۱۵۶ نمبر ۹۷۰) اس اثر میں ہے کہ حضرت عمرؓ تکبیر تشریق کہا کرتے تھے۔ اور یہ مسافر تھے پھر بھی تکبیر کہی (۳) دسویں ذی الحجہ کے عصر تک تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن ابی وائل عن عبد الله ابن مسعود انه كان يكبر من صلوة الفجر يوم عرفة الى صلوة العصر من يوم النحر - (مصنف بن ابی هیپه ۴۱۴ تکبیر من ای یوم حوالی ای ساعته ج اول، ص ۴۸۸ نمبر ۵۶۳۳ البیھقی ، باب من استحب ان يبتدئ بالتمير خلف صلوۃ الصبح من يوم عرفة ، ج ثالث ،ص ۲۳۹، نمبر ۶۲۷۴) اس اثر سے معلوم ہوا کہ ذی الحجہ کی نویں تاریخ کے فجر سے یوم النحر یعنی دسویں ذی الحجہ کی عصر تک تکبیر تشریق کہی جائے گی۔ (۴) اور جماعت ہو اور شہر ہو تب ہی تکبیر تشریق واجب ہے اس کی دلیل حضرت علی کا قول ہے ۔ قــال عـلـى : لا جمعة ولا تشريق ولا صلاة فطر و لا اضحى الا في مصر جامع او مدينة عظيمة - (مصنف ابن ابی شیبہ نمبر ۵۰۵۹/مصنف عبدالرزاق، نمبر ۵۱۹۱) اس اثر میں ہے کہ شہر کے علاوہ پر تکبیر نہیں ۔ ترجمه : (۸۳۶) اور صاحبین نے فرمایا کہ ہر نماز کے فورا بعد چاہے اکیلا پڑھی ہو، اور چاہے مسافر ہو، اور چاہے گا ؤں میں ہو تیرہویں ذی الحجہ کی عصر تک ۔ اسی پر عمل ہے اور اسی پر فتوی ہے۔ تشریح : صاحبین فرماتے ہیں چاہے جماعت کے ساتھ پڑھی ہو چاہے اکیلا پڑھی ہو، شہر میں پڑھی ہو چاہے دیہات میں پڑھی ہو ہر آدمی پر فرض نماز کے بعد تکبیر تشریق واجب ہے۔ وجه : (۱) تنہا نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن عمرو عن الحسن قال : اذا صلى وحده أو في جماعة أو تطوع كبر - (مصنف ابن ابي شيبة ، باب ۴۳۳، فی الرجل يصلى وحده يكبر ام لا؟ ، ج ثانی ،ص ۶ نمبر ۲۸۲۹) اس اثر میں ہے کہ اکیلا نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے۔ (۲) اور عورت اکیلی نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن ابراهیم قال يحب للنساء أن يكبرن دبر الصلاة أيام التشريق - مصنف ابن ابي شيبة ، باب ۴۳۷ ، فی النساء لیمن تکبیر أيام
Chapter of the Two Eids. (834) And al-ta'rif is nothing. (835) Takbir al-tashriq is obligatory from after Fajr of Arafa until Asr of Eid, once immediately after every fard prayer offered in congregation, according to Abu Hanifa. ... Translation: (834) And ta'rif is nothing. Explanation: Just as pilgrims go to Arafat, similarly people used to take the sacrifice animal to the field, which is called ta'rif. It has no status because these are acts of worship in the field of Arafat; elsewhere they have no status. Translation: (835) Takbir al-tashriq is obligatory from Fajr of the day of Arafa until Asr of Eid, once after every fard prayer that is recommended to be performed in congregation, upon the imam who is a resident in the city and upon the one who follows him, even if he is a traveler, slave, or woman, according to Imam Abu Hanifa. Explanation: ... They say it is obligatory every prayer immediately, even if prayed alone, even if a traveler, even if in villages, until Asr of the 13th of Dhu al-Hijja. This is what is acted upon and this is the fatwa.
Source pages p. 92

Commentary
This passage from Thamaratun Najah covers two legal topics related to Eid: the practice of ta'rif and the obligation of takbir al-tashriq. First, the author states that ta'rif—taking sacrificial animals to a field resembling Arafat—has no religious standing (laysa bi shay'). The commentary explains that this imitation of Hajj rituals is invalid outside of Arafat. Then the main discussion on takbir al-tashriq begins. The matn states two positions: Imam Abu Hanifa's view that takbir is obligatory only for those praying in congregation in a city, after each fard prayer from Fajr of 9th Dhu al-Hijja to Asr of 10th (Eid day). The Sahibayn (Abu Yusuf and Muhammad) hold it obligatory for every person after every fard prayer, whether alone or in congregation, in city or village, from Fajr of 9th to Asr of 13th. The author notes that the latter is the operative position (alayhi al-fatwa). The commentary provides proofs for each view: Abu Hanifa uses the statement of Ali (RA) that takbir is only in a major city (misr jami'), while the Sahibayn use general practices of the Companions including Ibn Mas'ud and Ibrahim al-Nakha'i. The student should note that this is an intra-Hanafi dispute resolved in favor of the Sahibayn's more expansive view.

Key Terms
التعريف (al-ta'rif): The practice of taking a sacrificial animal to an open field on Eid, mimicking the Hajj ritual of standing at Arafat.
تکبیر تشریق (takbir al-tashriq): The prescribed recitation of Allahu Akbar after fard prayers from Fajr of 9th Dhu al-Hijja to Asr of 13th (according to the preferred view).
مصر جامع (misr jami'): A major city where congregational prayers, including Jumu'ah, are regularly held.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the mufta bihi (relied-upon) position in the Hanafi school, who is obligated to recite takbir al-tashriq?
A) Only the imam of a congregational prayer in a city
B) Every person after every fard prayer, regardless of congregation, residence, or travel
C) Only men praying in congregation
D) Only residents of Mecca and Mina

Key Takeaway
The relied-upon Hanafi position obligates takbir al-tashriq after every fard prayer, for everyone, from Fajr of 9th to Asr of 13th Dhu al-Hijja.

Salah — Prayer
intermediate
8 min
Takbir al-Tashriq: Ruling and Intra-Hanafi Dispute
Intra-Hanafi dispute on Takbir al-Tashriq obligation

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi mufta bihi ruling on Takbir al-Tashriq and explain the intra-Hanafi dispute between Abu Hanifa and the Sahibayn.

Core Idea
Takbir al-Tashriq is wajib for every fard prayer – the Sahibayn's view is the operative position.

This passage examines the difference of opinion within the Hanafi school regarding Takbir al-Tashriq—the additional takbirs recited after obligatory prayers during the days of tashriq. Imam Abu Hanifa considered it mustahab only for the resident imam and congregation, while his two students, Abu Yusuf and Muhammad al-Shaybani, ruled it wajib for everyone. The text presents proofs for both sides and then clarifies which position is relied upon for fatwa.

Guided Path
1
State the Hanafi position (Abu Hanifa's view)
Identify exactly what Abu Hanifa ruled: mustahab only for the resident imam of a city and those who follow him in congregation, not for individuals, travellers, slaves, or women.
This is the minority view within the school.
2
Identify the Sahibayn's opposing view
Recognize that the Sahibayn ruled it wajib for every person who prays any fard prayer, regardless of being alone or in congregation, traveller or resident, male or female.
This is the mufta bihi.
3
Analyze the proofs for each side
Follow the dalil presented: Abu Hanifa relies on the general verse, 'Umar's practice as a traveller, and 'Ali's condition of a city. The Sahibayn rely on Ibn Mas'ud's continuous practice, al-Hasan's statement for individuals, and Ibrahim's recommendation for women.
Notice how each side uses athar of the Companions and Successors.
4
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
The practical consequence: Under Abu Hanifa, only the imam and his followers in a city recite; under the Sahibayn, everyone recites after every fard prayer during the days of tashriq.
This difference matters for individual practice.
5
Identify the mufta bihi and tarjih
The text explicitly states 'به يعمل وعليه الفتوى' (according to this is practice and upon it is fatwa), adopting the Sahibayn's view. Thus, the operative ruling is wajib for all.
Tarjih is based on the strength of their proofs and later acceptance.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
باب العيدين
مستحبة عـلـى امـام مقيم بمصر وعلى من اقتدی به ولو كان مسافرا او رقيقا او انثى عند ابي حنيفة رحمه الله (۸۳۶) وقالا يـجـب فـور كل فرض على من صلاه ولو منفردا او مسافرا او قرويا الى
اس کے مقتدی پر ایک مرتبہ تکبیر تشریق کہے۔ چاہے مسافر ہو چاہے غلام ہو یا عورت ہوسب پر واجب ہے۔ اور اکیلا پڑھی ہو تو تکبیر پڑھنا واجب نہیں ہے۔
وجه (۱) تکبیر تشریق کا ثبوت اس آیت میں ہے . ويذكر وا اسم الله فی ایام معلومات على ما رزقهم من بهيمة الانعام ۔ ( آیت ۲۸ ،سورۃ الحج ۲۲) اس آیت میں جواللہ کا ذکر کرنے کے لئے کہا گیا ہے اس میں تکبیر تشریق بھی ہے۔ (۲) اس قول صحابی میں بھی اس کا ذکر . و كـان عـمـر يـكـبـر فـي قبـة بـمـنـي فيسمعه أهل المسجد فيكبرون و يكبر أهل الاسواق حتى ترتج منى تكبيرا و كان ابن عمر يكبر بمنی تلک الايام و خلف الصلوات ۔ ( بخاری شریف باب التکبیر ایام منی واذ اغدا الی عرفته ص ۱۵۶ نمبر ۹۷۰) اس اثر میں ہے کہ حضرت عمرؓ تکبیر تشریق کہا کرتے تھے۔ اور یہ مسافر تھے پھر بھی تکبیر کہی (۳) دسویں ذی الحجہ کے عصر تک تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن ابی وائل عن عبد الله ابن مسعود انه كان يكبر من صلوة الفجر يوم عرفة الى صلوة العصر من يوم النحر - (مصنف بن ابی هیپه ۴۱۴ تکبیر من ای یوم حوالی ای ساعته ج اول، ص ۴۸۸ نمبر ۵۶۳۳ البیھقی ، باب من استحب ان يبتدئ بالتمير خلف صلوۃ الصبح من يوم عرفة ، ج ثالث ،ص ۲۳۹، نمبر ۶۲۷۴) اس اثر سے معلوم ہوا کہ ذی الحجہ کی نویں تاریخ کے فجر سے یوم النحر یعنی دسویں ذی الحجہ کی عصر تک تکبیر تشریق کہی جائے گی۔ (۴) اور جماعت ہو اور شہر ہو تب ہی تکبیر تشریق واجب ہے اس کی دلیل حضرت علی کا قول ہے ۔ قــال عـلـى : لا جمعة ولا تشريق ولا صلاة فطر و لا اضحى الا في مصر جامع او مدينة عظيمة - (مصنف ابن ابی شیبہ نمبر ۵۰۵۹/مصنف عبدالرزاق، نمبر ۵۱۹۱) اس اثر میں ہے کہ شہر کے علاوہ پر تکبیر نہیں ۔ ترجمه : (۸۳۶) اور صاحبین نے فرمایا کہ ہر نماز کے فورا بعد چاہے اکیلا پڑھی ہو، اور چاہے مسافر ہو، اور چاہے گا ؤں میں ہو تیرہویں ذی الحجہ کی عصر تک ۔ اسی پر عمل ہے اور اسی پر فتوی ہے۔
تشریح : صاحبین فرماتے ہیں چاہے جماعت کے ساتھ پڑھی ہو چاہے اکیلا پڑھی ہو، شہر میں پڑھی ہو چاہے دیہات میں پڑھی ہو ہر آدمی پر فرض نماز کے بعد تکبیر تشریق واجب ہے۔
وجه : (۱) تنہا نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن عمرو عن الحسن قال : اذا صلى وحده أو في جماعة أو تطوع كبر - (مصنف ابن ابي شيبة ، باب ۴۳۳، فی الرجل يصلى وحده يكبر ام لا؟ ، ج ثانی ،ص ۶ نمبر ۲۸۲۹) اس اثر میں ہے کہ اکیلا نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے۔ (۲) اور عورت اکیلی نماز پڑھے تب بھی تکبیر کہے اسکی دلیل یہ اثر ہے۔ عن ابراهیم قال يحب للنساء أن يكبرن دبر الصلاة أيام التشريق - مصنف ابن ابي شيبة ، باب ۴۳۷ ، فی النساء لیمن تکبیر أيام
عصر الخامس من يوم عرفة وبه يعمل وعليه الفتوى
Chapter of the Two Eids. It is recommended upon an imam residing in a city and upon whoever follows him, even if he is a traveller, a slave, or a woman, according to Abu Hanifa (may Allah have mercy on him) (836). And both (Abu Yusuf and Muhammad) said: It is obligatory immediately after every obligatory prayer upon whoever prays it, even if alone, a traveller, or a villager, until… Upon his follower, recite the takbir al-tashriq once. Whether traveller, slave, or woman, it is obligatory upon all. And if one prays alone, reciting takbir is not obligatory. Proof (1): The evidence for takbir al-tashriq is in this verse: 'And mention the name of Allah on known days over what He has provided them of grazing livestock' (Surah al-Hajj 22:28). This verse commands the remembrance of Allah, which includes takbir al-tashriq. (2) It is also mentioned in this statement of a Companion: 'Umar used to recite takbir in a tent in Mina, and the people of the mosque would hear him and recite takbir, and the people of the marketplaces would recite takbir, until Mina would tremble with takbir. And Ibn 'Umar used to recite takbir in Mina on those days and after prayers.' (Sahih al-Bukhari, Chapter of Takbir during the Days of Mina and when going out to 'Arafat, p. 156, no. 970) This athar shows that 'Umar used to recite takbir al-tashriq and he was a traveller yet he recited it. (3) He recites takbir until the 'Asr of the 10th of Dhul-Hijjah. The evidence for this is the athar: From Abu Wa'il from 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud that he used to recite takbir from the Fajr prayer of the Day of 'Arafah until the 'Asr prayer of the Day of Nahr. (Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah? 414, takbir from which day? volume 1, p. 488, no. 5633; al-Bayhaqi, chapter of one who recommended starting with... after Fajr of 'Arafah, volume 3, p. 239, no. 6274) This athar indicates that takbir al-tashriq is recited from the Fajr of the 9th of Dhul-Hijjah to the 'Asr of the 10th of Dhul-Hijjah. (4) Takbir al-tashriq is obligatory only when there is a congregation and a city. The evidence is the statement of 'Ali: 'Ali said: There is no Jumu'ah, no tashriq, no 'Eid al-Fitr prayer, and no 'Eid al-Adha prayer except in a congregational city or a great metropolis.' (Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah, no. 5059; Musannaf 'Abd al-Razzaq, no. 5191) This athar indicates that there is no takbir outside the city. Translation: (836) And the two Sahibayn said: Immediately after every prayer, whether one prays alone, is a traveller, or in a village, until the 'Asr of the 13th of Dhul-Hijjah. According to this is practice and upon it is fatwa. Explanation: The two Sahibayn say: Whether one prays in congregation or alone, in a city or village, every person must recite takbir al-tashriq after the obligatory prayer. Proof (1): Even if he prays alone, he still recites takbir. The evidence is this athar: From 'Amr from al-Hasan, he said: When he prays alone or in congregation or a supererogatory prayer, he recites takbir. (Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah, chapter 433, concerning the man who prays alone – should he recite takbir or not? volume 2, p. 6, no. 2829) This athar indicates that even if he prays alone, he still recites takbir. (2) And if a woman prays alone, she still recites takbir. The evidence is this athar: From Ibrahim, he said: It is recommended for women to recite takbir after the prayer during the days of tashriq. (Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah, chapter 437, concerning women – should they recite takbir during the days? ...) 'Asr of the fifth day from the Day of 'Arafah, and according to this is practice and fatwa.
Source pages p. 93

Commentary
This passage is an intra-Hanafi dispute (ikhtilaf) between Imam Abu Hanifa and the two Sahibayn (Imam Abu Yusuf and Imam Muhammad al-Shaybani) regarding the ruling of takbir al-tashriq—the additional takbirs recited after the obligatory prayers during the days of tashriq (11th, 12th, and 13th of Dhul-Hijjah). The author begins by stating Abu Hanifa's position: it is mustahab (recommended) only for the resident imam of a city and those who follow him in congregation. It is not obligatory for individuals, travellers, slaves, or women. Then he presents the Sahibayn's view: it is wajib (obligatory) for every person who performs any obligatory prayer, regardless of being alone or in congregation, traveller or resident, urban or rural, and including women and slaves. The passage then provides proofs for both sides. For Abu Hanifa's view: (1) The verse 'And mention Allah on known days' is general and not specific to takbir. (2) The practice of 'Umar ibn al-Khattab (ra) who was a traveller and he still recited takbir, but that does not prove obligation. (3) The statement of 'Ali (ra) restricting takbir to a major city. For the Sahibayn's view: (1) The practice of 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud from Fajr of 9th to 'Asr of 13th. (2) The statement of al-Hasan that one recites takbir whether alone or in congregation. (3) The recommendation for women to recite takbir. The author then clarifies that the mufta bihi (relied-upon position for fatwa) is the Sahibayn's view: takbir al-tashriq is wajib for everyone who performs a fard prayer, from the Fajr of the 9th to the 'Asr of the 13th of Dhul-Hijjah. This is the operative ruling in the Hanafi school.

Key Terms
تكبير التشريق (takbir al-tashriq): The additional takbirs recited after the obligatory prayers from Fajr of 9th Dhul-Hijjah to 'Asr of 13th Dhul-Hijjah, specifically during the days of tashriq.
مصر (misr): A large city or town where congregational prayers are established, as opposed to a small village or rural area.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the mufta bihi position in the Hanafi school, what is the ruling of Takbir al-Tashriq?
A) Mustahab (recommended) according to both Abu Hanifa and the Sahibayn
B) Wajib (obligatory) for everyone who performs a fard prayer
C) Wajib only for the imam and those in congregation in a city
D) Not prescribed at all

Key Takeaway
Takbir al-Tashriq is wajib after every fard prayer during the days of tashriq for all Muslims, regardless of gender, travel, or congregation, based on the Sahibayn's position which is the relied-upon view in the Hanafi school.

Takbir after Eid Prayers: Ruling and Wording
States the permissibility of takbir after Eid prayers and gives its wording

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the ruling on takbir after Eid prayers and identify its evidence from the Sunnah.

Core Idea
Takbir after Eid is mustahab, not wajib, and has a specific recommended wording.

After the joy of Eid prayer, many Muslims recite takbir. This lesson clarifies the ruling according to the Hanafi school: it is permissible and recommended (mustahab). We will examine the textual evidence and the wording taught by the Prophet's practice.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
Read the statement: 'لا بأس بالتكبير عقب صلوة العيدين'. The phrase 'la ba'sa' means no harm, which in Hanafi fiqh indicates permissibility, often rising to recommendation (mustahab) in acts of worship.
The ruling is not wajib but mustahab.
2
Analyze the first evidence
The hadith from Sunan al-Bayhaqi: the Prophet began with prayer and liked to recite takbir in the khutbah. Qiyas extends this to reciting takbir after the prayer itself.
The hadith is mursal (from 'Umar ibn Hafs) but accepted in this context.
3
Analyze the second evidence
The practice of 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud: he recited takbir nine times in the Eid khutbah. This qawl sahabi supports the recommendation.
Companion practice is a valid secondary proof in Hanafi usul.
4
Learn the recommended wording
The text provides the specific wording: 'Allahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, La ilaha illa Allah, Wallahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, wa lillahi al-hamd'. This is the masnun wording.
Other wordings are also permissible, but this is preferred.
5
Distinguish from takbir al-tashriq
Takbir al-tashriq is recited after fard prayers from Fajr of 9 Dhul Hijjah to Asr of 13th. This takbir is specifically after the Eid prayer itself.
Common confusion: ensure not to mix the two.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
(۸۳۷) ولا بأس بالتكبير عقب صلوة العيدين والتكبير ان يقول الله اكبر الله اكبر لا اله الا الله والله اكبر الله اكبر ولله الحمد .
تشريح : عید الفطر اور عیدالاضحی کی نماز کے بعد تکبیر کہنے میں کوئی حرج نہیں ہے۔
وجه : (۱) عمر بن حفص عن ابائهم عن اجدادهم ان رسول الله الله كان يبدأ بالصلاة قبل الخطبة و كان يحب ان يكبر التكبير بين اضعاف الخطبة ( سنن بیہقی ، باب التكبير في الخطبة فی العیدین، ج ثالث ص ۴۲۰، نمبر ۶۲۱۴) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ خطبے میں تکبیر کہتے ، جس کا مطلب ہوا کہ نماز کے بعد تکبیر تشریق کہہ سکتا ہے۔ (۲) عن مسروق قال كان عبـد الـلـه يـكـبـر في العيدين تسعا تسعا يفتتح بالتكبير و يختم به ـ ( سنن بیہقی ، باب التكبير في الخطبة في العیدین، ج ثالث ص ۴۲۰، نمبر ۶۲۱۵) اس قول صحابی میں بھی خطے میں نونو مرتبہ تکبیر کا ذکر ہے۔
اور تکبیر اس طرح کہے: اللہ اکبر الله اكبر لا اله الا الله والله اكبر الله اكبر ولله الحمد
(837) And there is no harm in reciting takbir after the two Eid prayers. And the takbir is to say: Allahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, La ilaha illa Allah, Wallahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, wa lillahi al-hamd. Explanation: There is no objection to reciting takbir after the prayers of Eid al-Fitr and Eid al-Adha. Evidence: (1) 'Umar ibn Hafs from their fathers from their grandfathers that the Messenger of Allah (s) used to begin the prayer before the khutbah, and he liked to recite takbir during the khutbah. (Sunan al-Bayhaqi, chapter of takbir in the khutbah of the two Eids, volume 3, p. 420, no. 6214) This hadith indicates that takbir was recited in the khutbah, meaning one can recite takbir after the prayer. (2) From Masruq, he said: 'Abdullah (ibn Mas'ud) used to recite takbir on the two Eids nine times, opening with takbir and closing with it. (Sunan al-Bayhaqi, same chapter, no. 6215) This statement of the Companion also mentions nine takbirs in the khutbah. And the takbir is to say: Allahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, La ilaha illa Allah, Wallahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, wa lillahi al-hamd.
Source pages p. 94

Commentary
This passage is a ruling regarding the permissibility of reciting takbir (the specific formula) after the two Eid prayers (Eid al-Fitr and Eid al-Adha). The author states that there is no harm (la ba's) in doing so, indicating it is permissible (mubah) or recommended (mustahab). The preferred wording is given: 'Allahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, La ilaha illa Allah, Wallahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, wa lillahi al-hamd.' The commentary then provides proofs: (1) A hadith from the Prophet (s) that he would recite takbir during the Eid khutbah, which implies it is also done after the prayer. (2) The practice of 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud (ra) who recited takbir nine times in the Eid khutbah. These evidences show the legitimacy of takbir in connection with Eid prayers. The takbir here is distinct from takbir al-tashriq, which is recited after fard prayers during the days of tashriq. This takbir is specifically for after the Eid prayer itself.

Key Terms
تكبير العيدين (takbir al-'idayn): The specific takbir recited after the two Eid prayers, with the wording given in the text.

Key Terms from Source Passage

B) Haram (forbidden)
C) La ba's (no harm, i.e., permissible/recommended)
D) Makruh (disliked)

Key Takeaway
Reciting takbir after Eid prayers is a recommended practice (mustahab) supported by the Prophet's example and companion practice, with a specific wording preferred.

Eclipse Prayer: Ruling and Procedure
Defines the eclipse prayer as sunnah with specific conditions

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on the eclipse prayer and identify its key procedural elements.

Core Idea
The eclipse prayer is sunnah, two rak'ahs like nafl, with one ruku' per rak'ah, led by the imam without adhan or loud recitation.

This lesson covers the basic ruling and procedure of the solar and lunar eclipse prayer according to the Hanafi school. We will see that it is a sunnah prayer performed in congregation, similar to nafl, with specific announcements and without the usual elements of fard prayers.

Guided Path
1
Identify the act and its ruling
Recognize that the eclipse prayer (salat al-kusuf/khusuf) is sunnah, not wajib or fard.
The text opens with 'سُنَّ' (sunnah).
2
List the conditions for validity
The prayer requires the presence of an imam or his deputy to lead the congregation.
Conditions (shurut) are external to the prayer's performance.
3
Identify the pillars (arkan)
The prayer consists of two rak'ahs, each with one ruku' and silent recitation, like nafl.
Unlike the Shafi'i school, Hanafi does not have two ruku' per rak'ah.
4
Note the sunan (recommended elements)
The announcement 'as-salatu jamiah' is used instead of adhan/iqamah, and congregation is sunnah.
There is no loud recitation and no khutbah.
5
Distinguish from fard prayers
Note the absence of adhan, iqamah, loud recitation, and sermon, which are typical for fard congregational prayers.
This highlights the supererogatory nature of the eclipse prayer.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
باب صلوة الكسوف والخسوف والافزاع
(۸۳۸) سُنَّ ركعتان كهيئة النفل للكسوف بامام الجمعة او مامور السلطان بلا اذان ولا اقامة ولا جهر ولا خطبة ولكن ينادى الصلاة جامعة .
فصل: سورج گرہن اور چاند گرہن وغیرہ نماز کے بیان میں
ترجمه : (۸۳۸) سورج گرہن کے لئے دور کعات سنت ہے نفل کی طرح جمعہ کا امام ہو یا بادشاہ کا مامور ہو۔ بغیر اذان اور بغیر اقامت کے، بغیر جہری قرآت کے اور خطبہ نہ ہو، بلکہ الصلاۃ جامعۃ کا اعلان کرے۔
تشریح : سورج گرہن کی نماز نفل کی طرح نماز پڑھانے کا مطلب یہ ہے کہ ایک رکعت میں دور کوع نہیں ہوں گے، بلکہ نفل کی طرح ایک ہی رکوع ہوگا۔ امام شافعی کے نزدیک حدیث کی بنا پر سورج گرہن کے ہر رکعت میں دور کوع ہوں گے۔ اور اس نماز کو امام یا سلطان کا جو ماً مور ہے وہ قائم کریں ۔ اس دور میں اکثر ملکوں میں سلطان نہیں ہے اس لئے مسجد کے امام نماز پڑھاتے ہیں۔
Chapter of the Prayer for Solar Eclipse, Lunar Eclipse, and Calamities. (838) Two rak'ahs are sunnah in the manner of nafl for the eclipse, with the Friday imam or the appointee of the sultan, without adhan, without iqamah, without loud recitation, without khutbah, but one announces: 'as-salatu jamiah'. Section: Regarding the prayer for solar eclipse, lunar eclipse, etc. Translation: (838) For solar eclipse, two rak'ahs are sunnah like nafl, whether the imam of Jumu'ah or the sultan's appointee, without adhan and without iqamah, without loud recitation, and no khutbah, but he announces 'as-salatu jamiah'. Explanation: The meaning of leading the eclipse prayer like nafl is that there will not be two bowings in one rak'ah; rather, like nafl, there will be only one bowing. According to Imam al-Shafi'i, based on hadith, there are two bowings in each rak'ah of the solar eclipse prayer. This prayer is established by the imam or the sultan's appointee. In this era, most countries do not have a sultan, so the imam of the mosque leads the prayer.
Source pages p. 94

Commentary
This passage is a ruling statement regarding the solar and lunar eclipse prayer. The author states that it is sunnah to pray two rak'ahs in the manner of nafl (voluntary prayer). This means each rak'ah has only one ruku', unlike the Shafi'i view which has two ruku' per rak'ah. The prayer should be led by either the Friday imam or an appointee of the sultan (ruler). It is done without the call to prayer (adhan) or iqamah, without reciting the Qur'an aloud, and without a khutbah (sermon). Instead, the congregation is gathered by announcing 'as-salatu jamiah' (prayer is gathering). The commentary clarifies that in the absence of a sultan, the local imam leads the prayer. This reflects the Hanafi position that the eclipse prayer is a supererogatory (nafl) congregation prayer, not a wajib or fard.

Key Terms
صلاة الكسوف (salat al-kusuf): The prayer performed during a solar eclipse, consisting of two rak'ahs like nafl.
الصلاة جامعة (as-salatu jamiah): An announcement to gather for prayer, used instead of adhan for eclipse prayer and other special occasions.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi school, how many ruku' are performed in each rak'ah of the solar eclipse prayer?
A) Two ruku'
B) One ruku'
C) Three ruku'
D) None, it is only supplication

Key Takeaway
The eclipse prayer is a confirmed sunnah performed in congregation without adhan or loud recitation, like nafl with one ruku' per rak'ah.

Ruling on Takbir After Eid Prayers
Ruling on permissibility and wording of Takbir after Eid

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on Takbir after Eid prayers as mustahabb and identify its prescribed wording and proofs.

Core Idea
Takbir after Eid is a recommended practice confirmed by the Prophet's action and companions' example.

This passage clarifies the permissibility and desirability of reciting Takbir after the Eid prayers. It also provides the specific wording and cites multiple proofs from the Prophet and his companions, establishing the practice as mustahabb (recommended) in the Hanafi school.

Guided Path
1
Identify the ruling expression
Locate the phrase 'لا بأس' which indicates permissibility and recommendation, not obligation.
This is a common indicator for mustahabb.
2
Extract the prescribed wording
The text provides a specific formula: 'Allahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, la ilaha illa Allah, wallahu Akbar, Allahu Akbar, wa lillahil hamd.'
Memorize this wording as it is the relied-upon formula.
3
Analyze the proofs
Three proofs are cited: the practice of Maimunah, a hadith about the Prophet's Takbir during the sermon, and the practice of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud.
Each proof supports the legitimacy and form of the Takbir.
4
Classify the hukm
Combine the ruling expression with the proofs to determine the Hanafi classification: mustahabb (recommended).
Distinguish from wajib/fard; the phrase 'لا بأس' shows it is not obligatory.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
ولا بأس بالتكبير عقب صلوة العيدين والتكبير ان يقول الله اكبر الله اكبر لا اله الا الله والله اكبر الله اكبر ولله الحمد . و كانت ميمونة تكبر يوم النحر . عمر بن حفص عن ابائهم عن اجدادهم ان رسول الله الله كان يبدأ بالصلاة قبل الخطبة و كان يحب ان يكبر التكبير بين اضعاف الخطبة . عن مسروق قال كان عبد الله يكبر في العيدين تسعا تسعا يفتتح بالتكبير و يختم به .

Source pages p. 94

Commentary
This passage presents the ruling on saying Takbir after the Eid prayers. The matn states 'there is no harm' (لا بأس), indicating it is permissible and recommended rather than obligatory. The specified wording (Allahu Akbar thrice, la ilaha illa Allah, etc.) is given. The commentary then brings three proofs: 1) the practice of Maimunah (the Prophet's wife) who would say Takbir on the day of sacrifice, 2) a hadith from the Prophet that he would say Takbir during the Khutbah (sermon), and 3) the action of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud who said nine Takbirs in the Eid prayer. These establish the legitimacy and form. In the Hanafi school, this Takbir is considered mustahabb (recommended), not wajib. It is sunnah to say it after the Eid prayer, and the wording provided is the preferred formula.

Key Terms
تكبير (takbir): The phrase 'Allahu Akbar' and the extended wording as prescribed
العيدين (al-‘idayn): The two Eids: Eid al-Fitr and Eid al-Adha

The Ruling on Eclipse Prayer: Sunnah Performed Like Nafil
Ruling and proofs for eclipse prayer

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling for the eclipse prayer and identify its key conditions, and explain why the Hanafi school holds one ruku per rak'ah.

Core Idea
Eclipse prayer is sunnah, not fard, performed like nafil with one ruku per rak'ah and silent recitation.

This passage establishes the ruling and manner of the eclipse prayer according to the Hanafi school. It clarifies that it is not an obligatory prayer but a sunnah, and provides the detailed method of performance. The text also cites multiple hadiths to support the position that it contains one ruku per rak'ah, contrasting with the Shafi'i view.

Guided Path
1
Identify the Act and Its Ruling
What is being ruled upon? What is the hukm level? The matn begins with 'سن ركعتان' indicating the act is two rak'at and the ruling is sunnah.
The term 'سن' (sunnah) is used, not 'فرض' or 'واجب'.
2
Locate the Dalil
The author adduces several hadiths: Abu Bakra, Qabisa, Samurah, Ibn Abbas, and Abdullah ibn Umar. Identify which are cited as primary proof.
The hadith of Abu Bakra is the first and strongest proof.
3
Trace the Wajh al-Dalalah
How does each hadith prove the ruling? For example, the hadith of Qabisa says 'صلوا كأحدث صلاة صليتموها من المكتوبة' implying one ruku per rak'ah like Fajr.
The absence of a second ruku in these narrations is taken as evidence that only one is sunnah.
4
Note the Ikhtilaf
The Shafi'i school holds that there are two ruku per rak'ah based on other hadith. Identify the dispute and the evidence each side uses.
The Hanafi response is that the two-ruku narrations are interpreted as additional actions but the default is one.
5
Evaluate the Hanafi Tarjih
The text implicitly prefers the Hanafi position by presenting these hadiths as proof. The mufta bihi in the Hanafi school is the view of one ruku per rak'ah.
The commentary states this is the standard Hanafi position.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
سُنَّ ركعتان كهيئة النفل للكسوف بامام الجمعة او مامور السلطان بلا اذان ولا اقامة ولا التشريق ولا جهر ولا خطبة بل ينادى الصلوة جامعة . عن ابي بكرة قال كنا عند النبي الله فانكسفت الشمس فقام رسول الله يجر رداءه حتى دخل المسجد فدخلنا فصلى بنا ركعتين حتى انجلت الشمس فقال النبي علم ان الشمس والقمر لا ينكسفان لموت احد فاذا رأيتموها فصلوا وادعوا حتى ينكشف ما بكم . عن قبيصة الهلالي قال كسفت الشمس على عهد رسول الله فخرج فزعا يجر ثوبه وانا معه يومئذ بالمدينة فصلى ركعتين فاطال فيهما القيام ثم انصرف وانجلت فقال انما هذه الآيات يخوف الله عز و جل بها فاذا رأيتموها فصلو اكاحدث صلوة صليتموها من المكتوبة . قَال سمرة بينما أنا غلام من الانصار نرمي غرضين لنا .... فصلى فقام بنا كاطول ما قام بنا في صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا قال ثم ركع بنا كاطول ما ركع بنا في صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا قال ثم سجد بنا كاطول ما سجد بنا في صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا ثم فعل في الركعة الأخرى مثل ذلك . عن ابن عباس قال : صليت مع رسول الله ليل عليه صلاة الكسوف فلم اسمع منه فيها حرفا من القرآن . وعن عبد الله بن عمر قال لما كسفت الشمس على عهد رسول الله نودي ان الصلاة جامعة .
Two rak'at like nafil are sunnah for the eclipse prayer, led by the Friday imam or the sultan's deputy, without adhan, iqamah, tashriq, loud recitation, or sermon, rather one announces 'al-salatu jami'ah'. From Abu Bakra: We were with the Prophet when the sun eclipsed, so the Prophet stood up dragging his cloak until he entered the mosque, and we entered, and he led us in two rak'at until the sun became clear, then said: 'Indeed the sun and moon are not eclipsed for anyone's death, so when you see them, pray and supplicate until what you have is removed.' From Qabisa al-Hilali: The sun eclipsed in the time of the Prophet so he came out agitated dragging his cloak, and I was with him that day in Madinah, and he prayed two rak'at making the standing long, then left and the eclipse cleared, and he said: 'These are signs by which Allah frightens His servants, so when you see them, pray like the most recent obligatory prayer you have performed.' Samurah ibn Jundub said: ... Then he prayed and stood with us longer than any prayer, we did not hear his voice, then he bowed with us longer than any bow, we did not hear his voice, then he prostrated with us longer than any prostration, we did not hear his voice, then he did the same in the second rak'ah. From Ibn Abbas: I prayed with the Prophet the eclipse prayer at night, and I did not hear from him any letter of the Qur'an. From Abdullah ibn Umar: When the sun eclipsed in the time of the Prophet, one announced 'al-salatu jami'ah'.
Source pages p. 94

Commentary
This passage details the ruling and manner of the eclipse prayer. The matn states that it is sunnah (سن), not fard, and is performed like a nafil prayer (one ruku per rak'ah). It is led by the Friday imam or an authorized deputy. It is without adhan, iqamah, loud recitation (jahr), or a formal sermon (khutbah). Instead, the announcement 'al-salatu jami'ah' (prayer is gathering) is made. The commentary then provides several hadith proofs: 1) Hadith of Abu Bakra shows the Prophet prayed two rak'at without mentioning two ruku, supporting the one-ruku view. 2) Hadith of Qabisa emphasizes praying 'like the most recent obligatory prayer' (Fajr), which has one ruku per rak'ah. 3) Hadith of Samurah explicitly describes one ruku per rak'ah and silent recitation. 4) Ibn Abbas confirms silent recitation. 5) Abdullah ibn Umar shows the announcement. A key intra-madhhab difference noted is that Imam al-Shafi'i holds two ruku per rak'ah based on other hadith, but the Hanafi position relies on these narrations. In practice, Hanafis perform one ruku per rak'ah, with silent recitation, and the imam or his deputy leads, and in the absence of a sultan, the local mosque imam may lead.

Key Terms
كسوف (kusuf): Solar eclipse
خسوف (khusuf): Lunar eclipse
الصلاة جامعة (al-salatu jami'ah): Announcement for eclipse prayer meaning 'prayer is gathering'

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi position presented, how many ruku are performed in each rak'ah of the eclipse prayer?
A) Two ruku in each rak'ah
B) One ruku in each rak'ah
C) Three ruku in each rak'ah
D) One ruku in the first rak'ah and two in the second

Key Takeaway
The eclipse prayer is a sunnah prayer performed like nafil with one ruku per rak'ah, without adhan/iqamah, loud recitation, or sermon, and announced by 'al-salatu jami'ah'.

Salah — Prayer
beginner
8 min
Core Rulings of Eclipse Prayer: Sunnah, Form, Call, and Recitation
Rulings and proofs for basic features of eclipse prayer.

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi ruling on eclipse prayer (sunnah mu'akkadah) and describe its specific features: no adhan/iqamah/khutbah, silent recitation, and the call 'al-salat jami'ah'.

Core Idea
Eclipse prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah: two rak'ahs, one bowing each, silent recitation, no formal call but 'al-salat jami'ah'.

In this lesson, we examine the foundational rulings of Salat al-Kusuf. The text begins by clarifying what this prayer does NOT include—no adhan, no iqamah, no khutbah—and then details the proper call and the mode of recitation. We will go through the textual evidence that establishes these rules as uniquely Hanafi.

Guided Path
1
Identify the three omissions
The text states that eclipse prayer has no adhan, no iqamah, and no khutbah. Understand why these are omitted (because it is not a congregational obligation like Jumu'ah).
Hanafi: these are not part of the prayer; the call is simply 'al-salat jami'ah'.
2
Identify the proper call
The call is 'al-salat jami'ah' (prayer is gathering). This replaces adhan and iqamah. The hadith of Ibn Umar confirms this.
3
Identify the recitation mode
Recitation is silent (sirr), not aloud. The Hanafi school relies on the hadith of Ibn Abbas that he heard no letter from the Prophet.
This contrasts with the Shafi'i school which prefers aloud recitation.
4
State the overall ruling
The prayer is sunnah mu'akkadah. The hadith of Abu Bakrah establishes this by the Prophet's action and command 'fasallu'.
In Hanafi usul, a command from the Prophet after a prohibition (here, the jahili belief that eclipses occur for someone's death) indicates recommendation, not obligation.
5
Note cross-madhhab difference
The Shafi'i school holds that eclipse prayer has two bowings per rak'ah and louder recitation. The Hanafi position is based on the absence of such in the primary reports and the analogy to Fajr prayer.
This is a legitimate ikhtilaf; the Hanafi view is mufta bihi in the school.

باب صلوة الكسوف
میں اذان بھی نہیں ہے اورا قامت بھی نہیں ہے، اور خطبہ بھی نہیں ہے، اور قرآت سری کرے جہری نہ کرے۔
وجه : (۱) عـن ابـی بــكــرة قال كنا عند النبى الله فانكسفت الشمس فقام رسول الله يجر رداءه حتى دخل الـمـسـجـد فـدخـلـنـا فصلى بنا ركعتين حتى انجلت الشمس فقال النبي علم ان الشمس والقمر لا ينكسفان لموت احد فاذا رأيتموها فصلوا وادعوا حتى ينكشف ما بكم. (بخاری شریف، باب الصلوۃ فی کسوف الشمس، ص ۱۴۱، نمبر ۱۰۴۰ / ابو داؤد شریف ، باب من قال اربع رکعات ،ص ۱۷۵، نمبر ۱۱۸۵) اس حدیث سے معلوم ہوا کہ سورج گرہن کے وقت نماز سنت ہے اور اس میں دور کوع کا ذکر نہیں ہے اس لئے ایک رکعت میں دورکوع نہیں ہوں گے۔اس میں اذان اور اقامت کا بھی ذکر نہیں ہے، اور جمعہ اور عیدین کی طرح با ضابطہ خطبہ بھی نہیں (۲) عن قبيصة الـهـلالـي قــال كسـفـت الشمس على عهد رسول الله فخرج فزعا يجر ثوبه وانا معه يومئذ بالمدينة فصلى ركعتين فاطال فيهما القيام ثم انصرف وانجلت فقال انما هذه الآيات يخوف الله عز و جل بها فاذا رأيتموها فصلو اكاحدث صلوة صليتموها من المكتوبة . (ابوداؤد شریف، باب من قال اربع رکعات ص ۷۵ انمبر ۱۸۵ رسن للبیھقی باب من صلى في الخسوف ركعتين ج ثالث ص ۲۶۴، نمبر ۶۳۳) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ فجر کی نماز میں جس طرح ایک رکوع کے ساتھ نماز پڑھی اسی طرح نما ز سورج گرہن کی پڑھی جائینگی۔ احدث صلوۃ من المكتوبة سے فجر کی نماز مراد ہے۔ نیز اس حدیث میں دو مرتبہ رکوع کرنے کا تذکرہ نہیں ہے (۳) سمرۃ بن جندب کی لمبی حدیث ہے۔ جس کا ٹکڑا اس طرح ہے ۔ قـال ســمــرة بينما أنا غلام من الانصار نرمي غرضين لنا .... فصلى فقام بنا كاطول ما قام بنا فى صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا قال ثم ركع بنا كاطول ما ركع بنا في صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا قال ثم سجد بنا كاطول ما سجد بنا في صلوة قط لا نسمع له صوتا ثم فعل في الركعة الأخرى مثل ذلك (ابوداؤد شریف، باب من قال اربع رکعات ص ۷۵ انمبر ۱۱۸۴) اس حدیث میں بھی اس بات کا تذکرہ ہے کہ ایک رکعت میں دور کوع نہیں کئے ۔ جس سے ثابت ہوتا ہے کہ سورج گرہن کی نماز میں ایک رکعت میں دور کوع نہیں کریں گے ۔ اس حدیث میں یہ بھی ہے کہ قرآت آہستہ کرے۔(۴) عن ابن عباس قال : صليت مع رسول الله ليل عليه صلاة الكسوف فلم اسمع منه فيها حرفا من القرآن . (مسند احمد، باب مسند عبد اللہ ابن عباس، ج اول ص ۲۸۳، نمبر ۲۶۶۸) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ قرآن کا ایک حرف بھی نہیں سنا، جسکا مطلب یہ ہے کہ سورج گرہن میں قرآت آہستہ پڑھی۔ (۵) اور الصلوۃ جامعہ ، کہہ کر اعلان ہو اس کے لئے یہ حدیث ہے . عن عبد الله بن عمر قال لما كسفت الشمس على عهد رسول الله ال نودی, ان الصلاة جامعة ، ۔ (بخاری شریف ، باب النداءب الصلاۃ جامعۃ فی الکسوف ص ۱۶۸، نمبر ۱۰۴۵) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ الصلاۃ جامعۃ ، کہے۔
(۸۳۹) وسُنَّ تـطـويـلهـمـا وتطويل ركوعهما وسجودهما
(۸۴۰) ثم يدعو الامام جالسا مستقبل القبلة ان شاء او قائما مستقبل الناس وهو احسن ويؤمنون على دعائه حتى يكمل انجلاء الشمس
لغت : الكسوف: سورج گرہن کو کسوف کہتے ہیں، الخسوف ، چاند گرہن کو خسوف کہتے ہیں الافزاع:خوف ،گھبراہٹ۔اس وقت نماز سنت ہے۔
ترجمه : (۸۳۹) مسنون ہے دونوں رکعتوں کو لمبی کرنا اور اس کے رکوع کو اور سجدوں کو لمبا کرنا۔
تشریح : مسنون یہ ہے کہ سورج گرہن کی نماز لمبی ہو، رکوع اور سجدے دیر تک ہوں تا کہ سورج کھل جائے۔ وجه: (ا) ان عائشة زوج النبي عل الله اخبرته ان رسول الله الله صلى يوم خسفت الشمس فقام فكبر فقرأ قراءة طويلة ثم ركع ركوعا طويلا ثم رفع رأسه فقال سمع الله لمن حمده وقام كما هو ثم قرأ قراءة طويلة وهى ادنى من القراءة الاولى ثم ركع ركوعا طويلا وهى ادنى من الركعة الاولى ثم سجد سجودا طويلا ثم فعل في الركعة الآخرة مثل ذلك ثم سلم وقد تجلت الشمس (بخاری شریف ، باب هل يقول كسفت الشمس او حسفت ، ص ۱۴۲، نمبر ۱۰۴۷ر مسلم شریف، کتاب الکسوف ،ص ۲۹۵، نمبر ۲۰۹۶) اس حدیث میں نما ز لمبی ہونے کا ذکر ہے ترجمه : (۸۴۰) پھر امام بیٹھ کر دعا کرے اگر چاہے تو قبلہ کی طرف رخ کر کے، اور چاہے تو کھڑا ہو کر لوگوں کی طرف چہرہ کرے، اور یہ زیادہ بہتر ہے، اور لوگ اس پر آمین کہیں ، یہاں تک کہ سورج کھل جائے ۔ تشريح : نماز کے بعد دعا کرے، پھر اس کی دو صورتیں ہیں [1] یا تو بیٹھ کر قبلہ رخ کر کے لوگوں کے لئے دعا کرے، [۲] دوسری صورت یہ ہے کہ قوم کی طرف رخ کرے اور کھڑے ہو کر دعا کرے۔
وجه : (۱) حدیث میں ہے ۔ عن ابی موسی قال خسفت الشمس في زمن النبي علي .... قال ان هذه الآيات التي يرسل الله لا تكون لموت احد ولا لحياته و لكن الله يرسلها يخوف بها عباده فاذا رأيتم منها شيئا فافزعوا الی ذکره و دعائه و استغفاره - (مسلم شریف ، باب ذکر النداء بصلاة الكسوف الصلاة جامعة ،ص ۱۳۶۹، نمبر ۱۹۱۲ ۲۱۱۷) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ اس قسم کی خوف کی چیز ہو تو دعا اور استغفار میں مشغول ہونا چاہئے (۲) عن ابي هريرة ...... فقال ان الشمس والقمر آيتان من آيت الله وانهما لا يخسفان لموت احد فاذا كان ذلك فصلوا وادعوا حتى يكشف ما بكم ( بخاری شریف ، باب الصلوۃ فی کسوف القمر ص ۱۴۵ نمبر ۱۰۶۳ر مسلم شریف ، باب ذکر النداء بصلاة الكسوف، الصلاة جامعة ،ص ۱۳۶۹، نمبر ۲۱۲۲/۹۱۵) اس حدیث میں ہے کہ نماز پڑھو اور اس وقت تک دعا کرتے رہو جب تک گرہن ختم نہ ہو ترجمه : (۸۴۱) اگر امام موجود نہ ہو تو لوگ اکیلے نماز پڑھیں۔ تشریح : امام نہ ہو تو الگ الگ پڑھنا واجب نہیں ہے، بلکہ یہ مصلحت کا تقاضا ہے،اس لئے اگر انتشار کا خطرہ نہ ہو تو یہ سب
Chapter on the Eclipse Prayer. There is no adhan, no iqamah, no khutbah, and recitation is silent, not aloud. Evidence: (1) From Abu Bakrah... (hadith). From this hadith it is understood that the prayer at the time of solar eclipse is sunnah, and there is no mention of two bowings in it, therefore there will not be two bowings in one rak'ah. Also there is no mention of adhan and iqamah, and there is no formal khutbah like Jumu'ah and the two Eids. (2) From Qabisah al-Hilali... (hadith). In this hadith, just as the Fajr prayer is prayed with one bowing, similarly the eclipse prayer will be prayed. 'Ahadath salatin min al-maktubah' refers to Fajr prayer. Also no mention of two bowings. (3) Long hadith of Samurah ibn Jundub... (hadith). This hadith also mentions that two bowings were not performed in one rak'ah. It also shows that recitation is silent. (4) From Ibn Abbas... (hadith). In this hadith, not a single letter of Quran was heard, meaning recitation in eclipse prayer is silent. (5) The announcement is made by saying 'Al-salat jami'ah'. The hadith of Ibn Umar says that 'Al-salat jami'ah' was called. (839) It is sunnah to lengthen them (the two rak'ahs) and to lengthen their bowings and prostrations. (840) Then the imam makes du'a, sitting facing the qiblah if he wishes, or standing facing the people, and that is better, and they say Ameen to his du'a until the eclipse clears. Lexicon: al-kusuf means solar eclipse; al-khusuf means lunar eclipse; al-ifza' means fear, panic. At that time, prayer is sunnah. Translation: (839) It is sunnah to lengthen both rak'ahs and to lengthen their bowings and prostrations. Commentary: It is sunnah that the eclipse prayer be long, with long bowings and prostrations until the sun clears. Evidence: (a) Aisha... (hadith). This hadith mentions the prayer being long. Translation: (840) Then the imam makes du'a, sitting facing the qiblah if he wishes, or standing facing the people, and that is better, and they say Ameen to his du'a until the sun clears. Commentary: After the prayer, he makes du'a. There are two forms: (1) sitting facing the qiblah and making du'a for the people, (2) facing the people and making du'a standing, which is better. Evidence: (1) Hadith of Abu Musa... (hadith) indicates that when such a fearful thing occurs, one should engage in du'a and istighfar. (2) Hadith of Abu Hurayrah... (hadith) says pray and make du'a until it is cleared. Translation: (841) If the imam is not present, the people pray individually. Commentary: When the imam is absent, praying individually is not wajib, but it is required by maslahah; therefore if there is no risk of disunity, all.
Source pages p. 95

Commentary
This passage is a ruling-with-proof from the chapter on Salat al-Kusuf (eclipse prayer). It begins by stating the foundational rulings: no adhan, no iqamah, no khutbah, and silent recitation. The author then provides five hadith proofs. The first hadith from Abu Bakrah establishes the sunnah nature and shows that only two rak'ahs are prayed with one bowing per rak'ah; no double bowing. The second from Qabisah confirms a single bowing by analogy to Fajr. The third from Samurah similarly affirms silent recitation and one bowing. The fourth from Ibn Abbas directly shows silent recitation. The fifth from Ibn Umar shows the call 'Al-salat jami'ah'. Next, ruling 839 states that lengthening the rak'ahs, bowings, and prostrations is sunnah, supported by Aisha's hadith of the Prophet's long prayer. Ruling 840 describes the imam's du'a after prayer: he may sit facing qiblah or stand facing the people (preferred), and the congregation says Ameen until the eclipse ends. Evidence from Abu Musa and Abu Hurayrah encourages du'a and remembrance. Finally, ruling 841 says if the imam is absent, people pray individually; the commentary clarifies this is not obligatory but recommended to avoid disunity.

Key Terms
الكسوف (al-kusuf): Solar eclipse; the sun's light being obscured.
الخسوف (al-khusuf): Lunar eclipse; the moon's light being obscured.
الصلاة جامعة (al-salat jami'ah): The call to gather for eclipse prayer, distinguished from adhan.
سنة (sunnah): In this context, a recommended act that the Prophet performed and encouraged.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
In Hanafi fiqh, what is the ruling on recitation during Salat al-Kusuf (eclipse prayer)?
A) It is recited aloud (jahr).
B) It is recited silently (sirr).
C) It is recited in a low voice except for the imam.
D) There is no recitation.

Key Takeaway
Eclipse prayer in the Hanafi school is sunnah mu'akkadah with two rak'ahs, one bowing each, silent recitation, and the call 'al-salat jami'ah'.
